	$('.more_items').hide();

<script> 
	var thisPage = 1;
	var prevPriceFrom;
	var prevPriceTo;
function setPrevPriceFrom(thisPrice) {  
	prevPriceFrom = thisPrice;
}  
function setPrevPriceTo(thisPrice) {  
	prevPriceTo = thisPrice;
}  
function getCookie(cname) {
    var name = cname + "=";
    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
    for(var i=0; i<ca.length; i++) {
        var c = ca[i];
        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length,c.length);
    }
    return "";
}
	var isViewAll = false;
originalPriceFrom = 0;
originalPriceTo = 100000;
function updateDataNew(pg,mode){  
	if(pg>1 && typeof titleTag !== 'undefined'){document.title = titleTag + ' page '+pg;} else if(pg==1 && typeof titleTag !== 'undefined') {document.title = titleTag;}; 
	if (pg==1) $('.more_items').hide();  
	thisPage = pg  
	pg2 = pg 
	
	var idstoCall='';
	var srtBy='';
	if  ((document.location.hash!="") &&  (document.location.hash!='#')) {
		var ids =[];
		for (i=0;i<document.location.hash.split("&").length;i++){
			tid = document.location.hash.split("&")[i].replace("#","").split("=")[0];
			if (tid=="pg"){
				pg2=document.location.hash.split("&")[i].split("=")[1]
			}else if (tid == 'srtBy') {srtBy=document.location.hash.split("&")[i].split("=")[1]} else { ids.push(tid) }
		}
		 ids.sort()
		 for (k=0;k<ids.length;k++){
			if (k>0){
				if ((ids[k].substring(0,2)==ids[k-1].substring(0,2)) &&(ids[k].substring(0,2)!='is')) {idstoCall= idstoCall +",";}
				else{idstoCall= idstoCall +",";}
			}
			idstoCall= idstoCall + ids[k];
		 }
	}
	if (mode!='append' && mode !='prepend') fadeBg(); else fadeBgEndless(mode);
	if (getCookie("Filters").indexOf("pz=10000")<0)
		$('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 'slow');
	if (srtBy!='') {srtBy = '&srtBy='+srtBy;};
	if (!isNaN($('#priceFrom').val()) && $('#priceFrom').val()!=0)
		var prevPriceFrom1 = $('#priceFrom').val();
	else
		var prevPriceFrom1 = originalPriceFrom;
	if (!isNaN($('#priceTo').val()) && $('#priceTo').val()!=0)
		var prevPriceTo1 = $('#priceTo').val();
	else
		var prevPriceTo1 = originalPriceTo;
	$.ajax({
	  url: '/ajax/cogr_esiajaxProxy.asp?c=FO_ProductsListResponsive&m=getResults&ws=ro-ro&pid=4'+ srtBy +'&catID=0&ids='+idstoCall+'&pg='+pg+'&st='+encodeURIComponent($('#searchText').val())+'&prices='+ $('#priceFrom').val() +','+ $('#priceTo').val() +'&BrandID=0&logged=&isNew=0&checkPoint=0verMo=1&CT=30m',
	  success: function(data) {
		$('#contentToUpdate').show();
		$('#fade').fadeOut();$('#fade').remove();
		$('.endless_loader').remove();
		if (data!='') {
		if (getCookie("Filters").indexOf("pz=10000")>=0 && pg>1) {
			runAjaxTrue = false;
			if(mode=='prepend') {
				$('.prod-list').prepend(data);
				$(window).scrollTop($('.pageNo_'+ pg).last().offset().top);
			}
			else
				$('.prod-list').append(data);
		}
		else {
			$('#contentToUpdate').html(data);
			runAjaxTrue = false;
		}
			setTimeout(function(){ prodList_prodEQ(); }, 500);
			setPrevPriceFrom(prevPriceFrom1);
			setPrevPriceTo(prevPriceTo1);
		}
		else {
			if (isNaN(prevPriceFrom)) prevPriceFrom = originalPriceFrom;
			if (isNaN(prevPriceTo)) prevPriceTo = originalPriceTo;
			BuildModalMessage('<h4>Mesaj</h4><p>Nu exista produse cu specificatiile selectate</p>');
			$('#closeModalMessage').click(function(e){
				resetFilters(prevPriceFrom,prevPriceTo,prevURL);
			})
		}
		QuickviewPopupEvent();
		$('.paging').click(function(e){
			e.preventDefault();
			var state = {},id ="pg" ,url = $(this).attr( 'rel' );
			state[ id ] = url;
			$.bbq.pushState( state );
		});
	  }
	});
	prevURL = window.location.href;
}function resetFilters(valA,valB,valC) {  
	if (valC.indexOf('#') != -1 && window.location.href!=valC) 
		window.location.href=valC; 
	if ($('#priceFrom').val()!=valA) 
		$("#slider-range" ).slider( "values", 0, valA ); 
	if ($('#priceTo').val()!=valB) 
		$("#slider-range" ).slider( "values", 1, valB ); 
	$("#slider-rangeAmount1" ).html(valA+'lei'); 
	$("#slider-rangeAmount2" ).html(valB+'lei'); 
}
function setCoo(pz){  
	if (pz == 10000)
		isViewAll = true;
	else
		isViewAll = false;
	$.ajax({
	  url: '/ajax/cogr_esiajaxProxy.asp?ws=ro-ro&pz='+pz,
	  success: function(data) {$.bbq.removeState( "pg" ); updateDataNew(1,0)  }
	});
}function setCooPhoto(mode){  
	$.ajax({
	  url: '/ajax/cogr_esiajaxProxy.asp?ws=ro-ro&photoMode='+mode,
	  success: function(data) {}
	});
}function setSrt(srt){  
	$.ajax({
	  url: '/ajax/cogr_esiajaxProxy.asp?ws=ro-ro&srt='+srt,
	  success: function(data) {
		$.bbq.pushState( "srtBy="+srt ); 
		$.bbq.removeState( "pg" );  updateDataNew(1,0); 
	}
	});

	var sliderId='slider-range';
	$("#slider-range").slider({
 	 range: true,
 	 min: 0,
 	 max: 799,
 	 values: [ 0, 799 ],
 	 slide: function( event, ui ) {
		var delay123= function() {
			$( "#"+ sliderId +"Amount1" ).html(ui.values[ 0 ] +"lei");
			$( "#"+ sliderId +"Amount2" ).html(ui.values[ 1 ] +"lei");
			$( "#"+ sliderId).parents('.filter').find('input').val( ui.values[ 0 ] +' - '+ ui.values[ 1 ]);
			var firstOffset = $("#"+sliderId).find('.ui-slider-handle:nth-child(2)').position().left,
			secondOffset =$("#"+sliderId).find('.ui-slider-handle:nth-child(3)').position().left,
			firstWidth = ($( "#"+ sliderId +"Amount1" ).width()/2),
			secondWidth = ($( "#"+ sliderId +"Amount2" ).width()/2)-5;
 	 	}
 	 	setTimeout(delay123, 5);

	});
